so this is just one example of a new era really in cognitive neuroscience where we're beginning to understand psychological processes like how you remember or imagine or even think in terms of the actions of the billions of individual neurons that make up our brains .	所以這只是一個新的認知神經科學的一個例子 , 我們開始了解心理的過程 , 像是你如何記得、想像 , 甚至在數十億個獨立神經元的行動中 , 開始思考 。
thank you very much .	非常謝謝大家
imagine a global security driven by collaboration among agencies , government , the private sector and the public . that's not just the distant hope of opensource fans , it's the vision of james stavridis , the supreme commander of nato , who shares vivid moments from recent military history to explain why security of the future should be built with bridges rather than walls .	想像一個全球安全驅動力 , 由政府、私營部門和大眾合作 。 這不僅僅是開放源碼的粉絲所驅動的遠景 , 最高層的namesstridis , 來自最近的軍事歷史中 , 維生下來的偉大時刻 , 來解釋為何未來的安全性應該是用橋而不是牆壁來建造的 。
collaboration , global issues , opensource , peace , politics , social media , violence , war	合作、全球議題、開放原始碼、和平、政治、社交媒體、暴力、戰爭、戰爭、開放原始碼、開放資源、和平、政治、政治、政治、社交媒體、社交媒體、暴力、暴力、
james stavridis: how nato's supreme commander thinks about global security	詹姆斯斯•斯特里迪斯:nato的最高指揮官對全球安全的看法是如何看待全球安全 。
i'm gonna talk a little bit about opensource security , because we've got to get better at security in this 21st century .	我將要談談開放原始碼安全 , 因為我們在21世紀必須更好 。
let me start by saying , let's look back to the 20th century , and kind of get a sense of how that style of security worked for us .	首先 , 讓我們回顧一下二十世紀 , 對於安全的運作方式 , 有點了解到安全的運作方式 。
this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the nato headquarters in belgium .	這是verdun , 法國的一個戰場 , 位在北美比利時總部的北方 。
at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	1916年 , 在verdun , 超過300天 , 70萬人死亡 , 每天大約2000人死亡 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	如果你將它推向20世紀的第二次世界大戰 , 你會看到史達林升級的戰役 , 300天 , 兩百萬人死亡 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們進入冷戰 , 繼續嘗試建造牆壁 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從第一次世界大戰開始 , 變成第二次世界大戰的馬吉尼線 , 然後我們進入冷戰 , 鐵幕 , 柏林牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	今天 , 我的論點是 , 與其建構安全 , 我們需要建立橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲有名的橋 。
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	它是一座橋 , 位於愛德華•安德里的小說 , 它談到如何在歐洲和巴爾幹半島 , 經過一段時間 , 一直有一座巨大的牆壁 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	最近 , 在過去十年 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 猶豫地 , 團結在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我認為 , 開放原始碼的安全性是要連結國際的 , 國際的介入 , 私人公開的 , 將它與戰略通訊聯繫在一起 , 主要是在社交網路上 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這樣做 , 因為我們的全球公有物在各方面受到攻擊 , 而沒有任何威脅的來源 , 都是由建牆來解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	很明顯 , 我是水手 。
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一艘線性 , 穿過印度洋 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	它的邊緣有協奏曲線 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	這是要防止海盜攻擊 。
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	海盜現在是世界上非常活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	海盜也非常活躍在馬拉加的位置上 。
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	它位於幾內亞海灣 。
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海看到它 。
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	在全球交通運輸系統中 , 它是10億美元的不連續性 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 當時有20艘船 , 500名海軍陸地主持人 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要考慮如何處理它 。
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	咱們來轉變一種不同的海洋 , 網路海 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這是兩位年輕男士的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	此時此刻 , 他們被監禁 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們進行了一張信用卡詐欺 , 用了超過一百億美金 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 在全球經濟中有2兆美元的連續性 。
two trillion a year .	一年兩兆美元 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	這只是英國的國內生產總值 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以這個網路海 , 我們知道無止盡是根本的開放 , 同時也受到威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	在全球公有物中 , 我擔心的另一件事 , 是人口販賣、毒品、鴉片、來自阿富汗的威脅 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心來自安地斯山脊的可卡因 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的運動 , 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的成本 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	人口販賣會在海上移動 , 但在全球公有物的其他地方 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴你們這是一個非常高科技的美國海軍陸戰隊我們用它來阻止人口販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是一個由毒品卡特爾負責的半個半個半個半個子 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	它是在南美的叢林裡建造的 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那低科技的火雞捕捉到它 , 它帶著六噸的可卡因 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	第四個 。 精密的通訊會掃描 。
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣、毒品、人、武器、上帝禁止大規模破壞的武器 , 是對全球公有物威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	今天我們一起在阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是在阿富汗的一個派對 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世界上百分之八十到九十的餅乾、鴉片和海洛因 , 來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	當然 , 我們也看到了恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是基地組織所在的地方 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個非常強烈的迫切性嵌在其中 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的關注也是全球公有物的一部分 , 我們必須解決的問題 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以 , 我們在這裡 , 21世紀 。
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們20世紀的工具不會有用 。
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我認為 , 我們不會只從槍枝的桶子上遞送安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不會只從槍枝的桶子上遞送安全性 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要軍隊的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這麼做時 , 我們必須要做得很好 , 且要有競爭力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關於國際、國際間、私人公共的關係 , 由網路上的策略通訊的概念所組成 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這如何以正面的方式運作 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都是拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 這很奇怪 。 我想我讀到 , 人口統計學 , 二十、三十歲的年輕男女 , 大部分都是在阿富汗的文盲 。 」
you would be correct .	你可能會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗安全部隊時 , 85%無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班長期在這些男人和女人都學會閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿著書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們在識字課程中讀書 , 透過和私人企業合作 , 和發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教過超過二十萬阿富汗安全部隊來閱讀和寫在基本的層面 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你閱讀和寫在阿富汗 , 你通常會把一支筆放在你的口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在儀式裡 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們把那支筆拿到很大的驕傲的錢 , 把它放在口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這使得國際組織有五十個國家參與這個任務 , 國際組織這些發展機構和私人公共機構 , 來進行這種安全 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教他們戰鬥技巧 , 但我認為 , 開放原始碼安全意味著將更長久的安全聯繫起來 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	它叫做舒適 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘叫做慈悲的姐妹船 。
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船隻 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這個 , 舒適 , 在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在典型的路易士 , 他們會進行四十萬個病人的治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它並不是由軍隊所組成 , 而是由人道組織組成的組合:營運希望、微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織發送志願者 。
interagency physicians come out .	外科醫生出來了 。
they're all part of this .	它們都是這個的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 帶著他的母親走兩天走進舒適的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他適應了 , 在他的極端的眼睛中 , 他突然抬起頭 , 說: 「 媽媽 , 維歐•埃爾普羅 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽 , 我看見這個世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	乘以四十萬人的治療 , 這種私人公開的合作 , 和安全部隊合作 , 你開始以非常不同的方式 , 創造安全的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	在這裡你可以看到棒球運動員 。
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在這張照片中挑出兩位美國軍隊嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	兩位年輕男孩兩位年輕男孩 。 這是一系列的棒球診所的一部分 , 我們探討了大聯盟棒球、國家部門 , 他們設立了這個防彈軍棒球員 , 他們是真正的軍隊 , 但參與這個使命的一部分 , 他們在拉丁美洲和加勒比海 , 在全美洲和加勒比海 , 在全美各個角落 , 創造了安全保險 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕男性和女性的榜樣 , 展現了關於健身和生活的典範 , 我主張幫助我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	另一方面 , 這種合作關係在災難性的解脫中 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍直升機 , 在2004年海嘯發生後 , 造成25萬人死亡 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些重大的災難中 , 2004年海嘯發生了25萬人死亡 , 2005年巴基斯坦的kamiri地震 , 8萬5千人死亡 , 海地震大約有30萬人死亡 , 最近的地震隧道加上了日本和核子產業 , 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際演員、國際關係、國際關係、私人合作合作 , 和安全的災難 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些是開放式安全的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它連接起來 , 越來越多的做法 , 像是這樣 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	各位現在看到的是這個想法: 「 啊 , 阿達密 , 這些必定是溝通的海道 , 或這些可能是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 , 這是全球根據推特的圖表 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 , 綠色是地緣化 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	它是一個絕佳的驅動人口調查 , 世界上六大國進行下降秩序:中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們要進入這些蚊帳 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	為什麼我們要參與其中 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們先前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	再舉一個例子 , 該如何傳遞這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦發表了一場這樣的演講 。 正如我對你們說的 , 我在facebook , 朋友們 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	聽眾笑了一下 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章是以ap來經營 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	世界上有兩個地方:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	頭條是:北約需求需求的朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上 , 我有數百個來自印尼的朋友請求 , 來自印尼人和芬蘭人 , 大多是說: 「 農夫 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 順便一提 , 哪個是北約 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	沒錯 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何傳遞訊息 , 移動那個訊息 , 是我們如何連結國際、國際、國際、私人公開、這些社會網絡 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我按下一個音 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在史考特的守衛中 。
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在阿富汗南阿富汗的監獄中 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我讓他來這裡提醒我們 , 我不想讓任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要有能力、有能力的軍隊 , 他們可以創造出真正的軍事效應 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這就是我們所做的核心 , 並且保護自由 , 言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍惜的事物 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道的 , 生命不是開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要軍隊 , 要不就在戰場上 , 要不就在戰場上 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會爭辯生命是一場災難 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你要把它撥進去 , 正如我在思考我們如何在21世紀建立安全性 , 我們要在真正的戰爭和危機上使用硬力 , 但還有很多例子 , 如我們今天所說的 , 軍隊可以成為創造21世紀安全、國際、國際、國際安全、私人公平、與競爭溝通的一部分 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我要說的是 , 今天早些時候我們聽到維基百科 。 我常常用維基百科來查證事實 , 就像你們所欣賞的 , 維基百科並不是由十二位傑出的人鎖在一個房間寫文章 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科每天都有成千上萬人輸入信息 , 每天有數百萬人用這些信息編排 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	對根本的觀點來說 , 沒有人像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有人像我們所有人一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的視覺陳述是非常簡單的:一個每個人都可以在知識總和分享的世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 透過結合國際、國際、私人公開、戰略溝通 , 在21世紀 , 我們就能創造所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常謝謝你們 。 謝謝 。
